 Despite several flaws, in 2015, the Air Force agreed to include Tejas aircraft in its fleet so that the Tejas program could continue and the Air Force could also deal with the ever-decreasing aircraft problem
 philhal tejas ko praarambhik parichaalan manjuuri (iosi) hi mili he or ab bhi ise antim parichaalan manjuuri kaa intjaar he
 Final operational clearance means the aircraft is fully ready for deployment
 sutron ne NDTV ko bataaya ki antim parichaalan manjuuri kabhi bhi mil sakati he
 Sources said that trivial issues now need to be resolved
 sutara ne bataaya, 'philhal vayusena payalton ko prashikshan dena or shaamil karnaa shuru karegi
 Also, test pilots joining the squadron will have to work closely with HAL to resolve minor issues
 ' In order to maintain sufficient number of aircraft, the Air Force has ordered 80 Tejas fighter jets, which will bring the total number to 120
 in vimaanon kii aapurti echeel kii utpaadan kshamta par nirbhar karegi
 The first fleet of 20 aircraft manufactured by HAL will not have air refueling capability which is necessary at any time of operation
 tippaniyan The next 20 aircraft will also be equipped with better radar and the ability to launch missiles beyond the visual range, an official said
 bharat in vimaanon main israeli radar kaa prayog karnaa chahta he
 The Ministry of Defense and HAL Tejas are in the process of increasing the production capacity of the aircraft
 yojana he ki kam se kam varsh main 8 vimaanon kaa utpaadan jarur kiya jaae jise badha kar 16 vimaan yani ek scawadran prati varsh kiya jayega

 unke rishtedaaron kii bhi rajya main kai rice milen hai, phir bhi vah kehete hai ki rice mil chalaanaa ghate kaa sauda he, or is dhandhe main tike rahanaa bahut kathin
 Shyamlal Aggarwal tells us, "nothing is left after the salaries we have to pay to the employees and the expenses incurred in running the electricity or running the mill
" 
 
 sarkaar ne hamen diya jane vaala milling charge pichley 10 saal se nahin badhaayaa he
 
 
 It is not easy for us to stick to this business
 
 
 " Despite Agarwal's agony, his business has flourished in the last few years and he has no intention of leaving it
 agarwal kii tarah bargad ke jaiprakash laat ne bhi chaaval ke kaarobaar main khub tarakkee kii he
 He says that he started with just Rs 65 and today he owns several rice mills
 vah kehete hai ki dhandha kathin he, lekin kaam chalaa rahe hai
 "there is loss or trouble in any business, but the successful man is the one who does business wisely
 
 
 " The government purchases 25 percent of the state's paddy in Bargarh district
 pichley kuch saalon main rice milon kii sankhya yahaan badhati hi rahi
 Today, where there are more than 1,000 rice mills in the entire state, in Bargarh their number has increased from four to 104 in the last decade
 lekin vidmbana yah he ki isi bargad main karz ke boj tale dabe kisaan lagaataar khudakushi karte rahe hai
 What is the truth of this contradiction? 
 
 ? disambar main sansad main rakhi gai sieji kii report kahati he 2009-10 se 2013-14 ke bich dhan kii kharid main kai gadabadiyaan huin
 
 
 This report shows that in the last several years, the rights of farmers were killed and the mill owners benefited illegally
 misaal ke taur par The government incurred a loss of 195 crores by giving the price of paddy transportation to the mill owners unnecessarily
 
 
 alag-alag rajyon main dhan se nikalne vaale chaaval ke anupaat ke bare main banaae gaye galat paimaane se bhi sarkaar ko 952 karod kaa nuksaan hua
 
 
 The CAG has said in the report that it is not known whether the amount of Rs 17,985 crore given to farmers in the name of support price actually reached them
 
 
 lekin sabase badi gadabadi dhan se nikalne vaale teen bai-products ko lekar he, jin par sarkaar mil maalikon se koi keemat nahin vasuulati
 The government gives money to the mill owners for paddy milling and the mill owners also get three by-products produced during the milling of the paddy
 ye bai-product hai
 
 
 Rice bran, which makes refined oil
 
 
 broken rice yaa kanaki, jo sharaab banane or pashu aahaar ke liye istemaal hota he
 
 
 Rice husk or husk, which is used to run boilers or make electricity
 
 
 sieji apni report main kahati he - bai-product se hone vaali kamai main khaasi badhotaree ke baavjood sarkaar ne mil maalikon ko die jane vaale milling charge ko saal 2005 se abhi tak nahin badla he
 This gave the mill owners an additional Rs 3,743 crore
 artiai kaaryakarta gaurishankar jain kehete hai ki is maamle main vah centre or rajya sarkaar se shikaayat karte rahe hai
 Gourishankar Jain told NDTV India, "the government took cognizance of my complaint and then the CAG investigation related to it has revealed a mess of thousands of crores of rupees
 sarkaar na keval mil maalikon ko rice bran, broken rice or bhusi se hone vaali kamai ko kai saal se andekha kar rahi he, balki mil maalik in bai-products se hone vaali kamai par koi inkam tex bhi nahin de rahe hai
 
 
 " udhar mil maalikon kaa kahana he ki agar ve bazaar main tike hai to keval bai-product se ho rahi aamadani ke dam par, kyonki sarkaar ne pichley kai saal se dhan kii kutai ke daam nahin badaye hai or aaj bhi prati quintal 20 rupee hi milling charge miltaa he
 On the other hand, the farmers say that the government is not paying attention to this
 bargad ke kisaan jeke sahu or pike ganpati kehete hai, "mil maalik to lagaataar amir ho rahe hai
 
 
 This business is earning so much that if you pick up the biodata of Bargad mill owners, then you will find that those who were modest people till a few years ago, they are not only mill owners today, but they have lots in metros like Delhi and Mumbai
 All property is also there
 
 
 "tippaniyan But government official Vijay Kumar Rath says that if the farmers are losing money and the mill owners are benefiting, it is only because of policy disturbances
 hamaara kaam mil maalikon ko dhan milling ke paise dena or unase 67 pratishat chaaval waapas lenaa he
 There is no system in the policy regarding the by-product
 so, bhale hi is kami ke liye nitigat gadabadiyaan zimmedaar hon, lekin yah bhi sach he ki jahaan mil maalikon ne bargad samet urisa or puure desh main ek bada samrajya khadaa kiya he, vahiin kisaanon ke liye haal har jagah kharaab hi hote gaye hai
 Shyamlal Aggarwal tells us, "nothing is left after the salaries we have to pay to the employees and the expenses incurred in running the electricity or running the mill
" 
 
 sarkaar ne hamen diya jane vaala milling charge pichley 10 saal se nahin badhaayaa he
 
 
 It is not easy for us to stick to this business
 
 
 " Despite Agarwal's agony, his business has flourished in the last few years and he has no intention of leaving it
 agarwal kii tarah bargad ke jaiprakash laat ne bhi chaaval ke kaarobaar main khub tarakkee kii he
 He says that he started with just Rs 65 and today he owns several rice mills
 vah kehete hai ki dhandha kathin he, lekin kaam chalaa rahe hai
 "there is loss or trouble in any business, but the successful man is the one who does business wisely
 
 
 " The government purchases 25 percent of the state's paddy in Bargarh district
 pichley kuch saalon main rice milon kii sankhya yahaan badhati hi rahi
 Today, where there are more than 1,000 rice mills in the entire state, in Bargarh their number has increased from four to 104 in the last decade
 lekin vidmbana yah he ki isi bargad main karz ke boj tale dabe kisaan lagaataar khudakushi karte rahe hai
 What is the truth of this contradiction?

 ye bai-product hai

 broken rice yaa kanaki, jo sharaab banane or pashu aahaar ke liye istemaal hota he
 
 
 Rice husk or husk, which is used to run boilers or make electricity
 
 
 sieji apni report main kahati he - bai-product se hone vaali kamai main khaasi badhotaree ke baavjood sarkaar ne mil maalikon ko die jane vaale milling charge ko saal 2005 se abhi tak nahin badla he
 This gave the mill owners an additional Rs 3,743 crore
 artiai kaaryakarta gaurishankar jain kehete hai ki is maamle main vah centre or rajya sarkaar se shikaayat karte rahe hai
 Gourishankar Jain told NDTV India, "the government took cognizance of my complaint and then the CAG investigation related to it has revealed a mess of thousands of crores of rupees
 sarkaar na keval mil maalikon ko rice bran, broken rice or bhusi se hone vaali kamai ko kai saal se andekha kar rahi he, balki mil maalik in bai-products se hone vaali kamai par koi inkam tex bhi nahin de rahe hai
 
 
 " udhar mil maalikon kaa kahana he ki agar ve bazaar main tike hai to keval bai-product se ho rahi aamadani ke dam par, kyonki sarkaar ne pichley kai saal se dhan kii kutai ke daam nahin badaye hai or aaj bhi prati quintal 20 rupee hi milling charge miltaa he
 On the other hand, the farmers say that the government is not paying attention to this
 bargad ke kisaan jeke sahu or pike ganpati kehete hai, "mil maalik to lagaataar amir ho rahe hai
 
 
 This business is earning so much that if you pick up the biodata of Bargad mill owners, then you will find that those who were modest people till a few years ago, they are not only mill owners today, but they have lots in metros like Delhi and Mumbai
 All property is also there
 
 
 "tippaniyan But government official Vijay Kumar Rath says that if the farmers are losing money and the mill owners are benefiting, it is only because of policy disturbances
 hamaara kaam mil maalikon ko dhan milling ke paise dena or unase 67 pratishat chaaval waapas lenaa he
 There is no system in the policy regarding the by-product
 so, bhale hi is kami ke liye nitigat gadabadiyaan zimmedaar hon, lekin yah bhi sach he ki jahaan mil maalikon ne bargad samet urisa or puure desh main ek bada samrajya khadaa kiya he, vahiin kisaanon ke liye haal har jagah kharaab hi hote gaye hai

 "tippaniyan But government official Vijay Kumar Rath says that if the farmers are losing money and the mill owners are benefiting, it is only because of policy disturbances
 hamaara kaam mil maalikon ko dhan milling ke paise dena or unase 67 pratishat chaaval waapas lenaa he
 There is no system in the policy regarding the by-product
 so, bhale hi is kami ke liye nitigat gadabadiyaan zimmedaar hon, lekin yah bhi sach he ki jahaan mil maalikon ne bargad samet urisa or puure desh main ek bada samrajya khadaa kiya he, vahiin kisaanon ke liye haal har jagah kharaab hi hote gaye hai
 As an example mil maalikon ko bevajaah dhan dhulaai kii keemat dene se sarkaar ko 195 karod kaa ghaataa hua
 
 
 The government also suffered a loss of 952 crores due to the incorrect scale created about the proportion of rice produced in different states
 
 
 sieji ne report main kaha he ki iskaa pataa nahin ki samarthan mulya ke naam par kisaanon ko di gai 17,985 karod rupee kii rakam asal main un tak pahunchi yaa nahin
 
 
 But the biggest problem is with the three by-products from the paddy, on which the government does not charge any price from the mill owners
 sarkaar mil maalikon ko dhan kii kutai ke liye paisa detii he or dhan kii milling ke vakt usase nikalne vaale teen bai-product bhi mil maalikon ko hi milte hai
 These are by-products
 
 
 rice bran, jisase rifind oil banaaya jaataa he
 
 
 Broken rice or kanki, used for making wine and animal feed
 
 
 rice hask yaa bhusi, jo boyler chalaane yaa bijli banane ke kaam aati he
 
 
 The CAG states in its report - Despite a significant increase in the earnings from the by-product, the government has not changed the milling charge paid to the mill owners since 2005
 isse mil maalikon ko 3,743 karod rupee kaa atirikt phayda hua
 RTI activist Gaurishankar Jain says that he has been complaining to the central and state government in this matter
 gaurishankar jain ne NDTV india se kaha, "meri shikaayat kaa sarkaar ne sangyaan liya or phir ise lekar jo sieji jaanch hui, usamen hazaron karod rupee kii gadabadi kii baat saamne ai he
 The government is not only ignoring the earnings made from rice bran, broken rice and husk for the mill owners for many years, but the mill owners are not paying any income tax on the earnings from these by-products
 
 
 " On the other hand, the mill owners say that if they are in the market then only on the basis of the income from the by-product, because the government has not increased the price of paddy milling for the last several years and even today only Rs 20 per quintal milling
 Get charged
 udhar kisaan kehete hai ki sarkaar is ore dhyaan hi nahin de rahi he
 Barkar farmers JK Sahu and PK Ganapathi say, "mill owners are constantly getting rich
 
 
 is dhandhe main itani kamai ho rahi he ki agar aap bargad ke mil maalikon kaa biodata uthaa len to pataa chalegaa ki jo kuch saal pehle tak maamuli log the, ve aaj na keval mil maalik hai, balki dilli or mumbai jaise mahanagaron main unke paas dher sari sampatti bhi he
 
 
 "comments lekin sarkari adhikari vijay kumaar rath kehete hai ki agar kisaanon ko ghaataa or mil maalikon ko phayda ho rahaa he to yah sirf nitigat gadabadi kii vajah se he
 Our job is to pay the paddy milling money to the mill owners and withdraw 67 percent of the rice from them
 bai-product ke bare main policy main koi vyavastha nahin he
 So, even though policy lapses are responsible for this shortage, it is also true that while mill owners have built a huge empire in Orissa and the entire country, including Bargad, the condition of farmers has worsened everywhere

 "comments lekin sarkari adhikari vijay kumaar rath kehete hai ki agar kisaanon ko ghaataa or mil maalikon ko phayda ho rahaa he to yah sirf nitigat gadabadi kii vajah se he
 Our job is to pay the paddy milling money to the mill owners and withdraw 67 percent of the rice from them
 bai-product ke bare main policy main koi vyavastha nahin he
 So, even though policy lapses are responsible for this shortage, it is also true that while mill owners have built a huge empire in Orissa and the entire country, including Bargad, the condition of farmers has worsened everywhere
 udhar mil maalikon kaa kahana he ki agar ve bazaar main tike hai to keval bai-product se ho rahi aamadani ke dam par, kyonki sarkaar ne pichley kai saal se dhan kii kutai ke daam nahin badaye hai or aaj bhi prati quintal 20 rupee hi milling charge miltaa he
 On the other hand, the farmers say that the government is not paying attention to this
 bargad ke kisaan jeke sahu or pike ganpati kehete hai, "mil maalik to lagaataar amir ho rahe hai
 
 
 This business is earning so much that if you pick up the biodata of Bargad mill owners, then you will find that those who were modest people till a few years ago, they are not only mill owners today, but they have lots in metros like Delhi and Mumbai
 All property is also there
 
 
 "tippaniyan But government official Vijay Kumar Rath says that if the farmers are losing money and the mill owners are benefiting, it is only because of policy disturbances
 hamaara kaam mil maalikon ko dhan milling ke paise dena or unase 67 pratishat chaaval waapas lenaa he
 There is no system in the policy regarding the by-product
 so, bhale hi is kami ke liye nitigat gadabadiyaan zimmedaar hon, lekin yah bhi sach he ki jahaan mil maalikon ne bargad samet urisa or puure desh main ek bada samrajya khadaa kiya he, vahiin kisaanon ke liye haal har jagah kharaab hi hote gaye hai
 But government official Vijay Kumar Rath says that if the farmers are losing money and the mill owners are benefiting, it is only because of policy disturbances
 hamaara kaam mil maalikon ko dhan milling ke paise dena or unase 67 pratishat chaaval waapas lenaa he
 There is no system in the policy regarding the by-product
 so, bhale hi is kami ke liye nitigat gadabadiyaan zimmedaar hon, lekin yah bhi sach he ki jahaan mil maalikon ne bargad samet urisa or puure desh main ek bada samrajya khadaa kiya he, vahiin kisaanon ke liye haal har jagah kharaab hi hote gaye hai
 So, even though policy lapses are responsible for this shortage, it is also true that while mill owners have built a huge empire in Orissa and the entire country, including Bargad, the condition of farmers has worsened everywhere
 mumbai main samaajawaadee party ke parshad rais shaikh ne food and drug administration(epad) or brihanmumbai mahanagarapalika(biemasi) se ek ajeebogareeb maang kii he
 He has requested the FDA and BMC to ensure the display of halal signs outside the restaurant
 bataa den ki halaal pashu vadh kii ek prakriya he jo musalamaanon ke liye anivaary he
 He said that this should be done so that Muslims can eat out without doubt in their mind
 bataa den ki shaikh ne musalamaanon ke liye pehle baar koi aisi maang nahin kii he
 Recently, he had said that during the operation in hospitals, the beard of Muslim patients should not be shaved
 unhone kaha ki main yah sab medical raay lene ke baad kah rahaa hum
 For this, he wrote a letter to BMC
 shaikh ke mutabik dharmik pahalu ke tahat jo bhi aata he,us par hamen dhyaan dena chahie
 He also referred to the constitution and said that the constitution gives us the freedom to obey and not obey religious customs
 shaikh ne kaha ki dadhi ko hataanaa anivaary nahin he
 You can cover it
 sarkari aspataal is bare main bahut asamvedansheel hai 
 Rais Sheikh believes that beard is an important part of Islam
 lekin wo khud isko nahin rakhte
 He said that it is not that every Muslim has a beard
 main muslim hum, lekin main reeti-rivaajon kaa paalan nahin karata
 So i do not keep
 unhone aage kaha ki iskaa matlab yah nahin he ki mujhe is mudde par baat karne kaa koi adhikaar nahin he
 i am speaking for the people i represent
 rashtriya rajdhani dilli main shanivaar subah koharaa chaaya rahaa

 kareeb 30 railgadiyon kaa parichaalan prabhavit hua he

 vahiin simanchal express bhi 18 ghanton kii deree se chal rahi he

 haalanki din main aasmaan saaf rahegaa

 chunki vitt vidheyak, dhan-sambandhi vidheyak hota he, isliye ise sirf loksabhaa dwaara paas kiya janaa zaruri hota he, or rajyasabha se paarit karwaane kii aavashyaktaa nahin hoti
 With the new fiscal year starting from April 1, some special rules related to income tax will be changed
 vitt mantri arun jetali ne bajet 2017 main inakam tex main kai badlaavon kii bhi ghoshnaa kii thi
 The Lok Sabha has approved some changes in the Finance Bill
 aise main aap bhi jaan lijie ki nae vitt varsh yani 1 april se kya kuch badalane vaala he: 1
 dhai lakh se 5 lakh rupee ke bich kii inakam waalon kaa tex 10 fisad se ghataakar 5 fisadi kar diya jayega
 However, the exemption of Rs 5000 under section 87A has been reduced to Rs 2500
 itnaa hi nahin, jin ykardaataaon kii aay 3
 Above 5 lakh rupees there is no exemption for them
 iskaa matlab yah hoga ki 3 se 5 lakh rupye kii karyogy aay waalon ko 7,700 rupye kii bachat hogi, jabaki 5 se 50 lakh rupye texable inakam waalon ko 12,900 rupye kii bachat hogi
 2
 50 lakh se lekar ek karod rupye tak kii vaarshik aay vaale logon ko 10 pratishat sarcharge dena hoga
 (at the same time, people with an annual income of one crore rupees will have to pay 15 percent surcharge as before
 ) 3
 paanch lakh rupye kii salanaa aay (vyavsaayik inakam ke alaava) vaale vyaktigat karadaataaon ke liye suvidha ke liye tex ritern file karne ke liye ek pej kaa form pesh kiya jayega
 4
 rajeev gandhi equity seaving skim main nivesh par akalan varsh 2018-19 ke liye kisi bhi prakaar kaa kar laabh nahin milegaa
 This tax saving scheme was announced in the financial year 2012-13
 yah yojana pratibhuti bazaar main pehali baar nivesh karne vaale niveshkon ko protsaahit karne ke liye shuru kii gai thi
 5
 yadi search oparation ke dauraan 50 lakh rupye se adhik kii aghoshit aay yaa sampatti kaa pataa chalata he to iskar adhikari pichley 10 saal ke kar maamalon ko dobaaraa khol sakate hai
 At present, the tax authorities have the right to scrutinize the documents of the last six years only
 samay par apana ritern file nahin karne vaale karadaataaon ko akalan varsh 2018-19 ke liye 10,000 rupye tak kaa jurmaana dena pad saktaa he
 However, if the total income of a person does not exceed Rs
 5 lakhs, then the maximum penalty on him under this section shall not exceed Rs
 1,000
 6
 For long term gains, the holding period of an asset has been reduced from 3 years to 2 years
 yadi koi vyakti sampatti kharidkar use 2 saal ke bheetar hi bech detaa he to use is par hone vaale laabh par short turm capital gen tex dena hoga
 If the property is sold after two years from the date of purchase, no tax will be payable on it
 7
 The government has reduced the tax benefit of renters
 maujuuda kar kanoon ke mutabik kiraaye par di gai sampatti ke liye karadaata rental inakam ko samyojit karne ke baad home lone par chukaaye jane vaale sampurna byaaj par tex katautee kaa laabh le saktaa he
 Now according to the new rule, the benefit of tax deduction will be given on the payment of interest on home loan for 2 lakh rupees for own house, but only after adjusting the taxpayer rental income for the property given on rent, at only 2 lakh rupees per year
 Tax will be able to benefit
 do lakh rupye se adhik kii raashi ko agle aath assesament varshon tak aage le jaaya ja sakegaa
 8
 pratimah 50,000 rupye se adhik ke kiraaye kaa bhugtan karne vaale vyakti ko ab 5 pratishat tids (strot kar kar) kaatna hoga
 Tax experts believe that with this step, people who have very high rental income will come under the tax net
 yah niyam ek june 2017 se prabhavi hogatippaniyan 9
 neshnal pension system (enpies) se aanshik nikasi / aaharan par koi tex nahin lagegaa
 As per the proposed changes, NPS subscribers will be able to withdraw 25 per cent of their contribution in an emergency before retirement
 yah yaad rakhen ki ritairement par kul fund kaa 40 pratishat hissaa hi kar mukt hota he
 10
 ek july se pan card banavaane or inakam tex daakhil karne ke liye aadhaar number anivaary hoga
 The government has also reduced the cash transaction limit from 3 to Rs 2 lakh for the prevention of black money
 yadi koi vyakti do lakh rupye se adhik kaa lenden karte paaya jaataa he to use is seemaa se adhik raashi par 100 pratishat jurmaana dena hoga

 We want to advance the country on the path of 'sabka Saath, Sabka Vikas' - congress party paraajay ke bhay se gathbandhan karne par aa gayi he
 Today, the Congress which crushed small parties under the influence of power is lying in the ranks of those small parties: PM Modi - ham dhan bal ke hisaab se chunaav naa to ladate hai or naa hi ladanaa chaahate hai, ham jan bal ke hisaab se chunaav ladate hai
 That is why our mantra is 'my booth - strongest': PM Modi - jis congress ne madhya pradesh or yahaan kii janata se dushmani rakhi ho use sajaa dene kaa mauka madhya pradesh kii janata ke paas aa gaya he : piem modi - PM Modi said that the party which is more than 125 years old, the party of which has many former governors, then what happened so that such a big party has to come out with microscopic instruments that are not left anywhere in the country and after so much defeat Even the Congress is not ready to improve
 - piem modi ne kaha ki madhya pradesh main agade-pichhadon kaa bodh desh kaa bhala nahin karegaa As long as there was a UPA government in Delhi, then he was sitting with a sense of enmity towards the state governments of the BJP and the people there: PM Modi - piem modi ne kaha ki ham dhan bal se nahin balki janabal se chunaav ladate hai
 - We are those who are accepted by Gandhi, Ram Manohar Lohia is also approved and Deendayal Upadhyaya is also accepted because we believe in coordination, social justice and everyone's support, development of all: PM Modi -hamaare desh main vot bank kii raajnneeti ne samaaj ko samaaj ko dimak kii tarah tabah kar diya he or isiilie azaadi ke 70 saal main jo barbaadi aayi usase agar desh ko bachaana he to hamaare saamne ye vot bank kii raajnneeti kii dimak se desh ko mukt ye bhaajapa kii vishesh jimmevary he : piem modi - Development of all is not just an election slogan
 ujjwal bharat ke liye, koti-koti bhartiya aashaa or aakankshaon kii purti ke liye soch samaj ke chunaa hua ye hamaara maarg he: piem modi - PM Modi said that contemplation of Pandit Deen Dayal Upadhyay, his life, his ethos, his thoughts are our inspiration even today

 - PM Modi said that after independence, the country can never forget the three great men, Mahatma Gandhi, Lohia and Pandit Deendayal Upadhyaya; These three took the country to new heights
 - piem modi ne kaha- BJP akeli party he jo maanavtaa ke mudde ko lekar raajnneetik jivan main kaa karti he It is a matter of pride for the BJP to have a government in 19 states but it is a matter of pride to be the world's largest party: PM Modi - ham kitne bhaagyashaalee he yaa hamanen naa jane kitne punya kiye honge ki hame is party (bhaajapa) ke madhyam se maa bharti kii seva karne kaa saubhaahgya praapt hua he : piem modi - PM Modi said that i see millions of people full of energy
